45. For all forms of the gods are but reflections of the Circle, and their miracles come from the living in them, and the living are from the Circle. There was no miracle that was not from the Circle; and he who is with the Circle is light in the darkness.
46. In every form of the god, the best is the smallest part of the Circle, the worst is the void, and there is nothing more in it, for the whole world is from the Circle and the void.
47. Draw the sign of the Circle above the forms of the gods, and you will see.
48. And when you speak to a man, speak to the Circle in him, and you will continue in the Circle; rejoice!
49. Behold, both the rich and the powerful, in measure of the Circle, possess wealth and power.
50. And in measure of the void, both wealth and power are but ashes and weeping.
51. They asked him: what about scriptures and faiths? He answered: You see what is in them from the Circle.
52. For all herds meet the butcher's knife at the end. But flocks of birds, flying towards the spring light, find continuation. The Circle is Light.
53. What then, will faith and form of the gods not enter the Circle? Truly, the void takes even from the form of the gods.
54. How many cunning words and crafty silences are there among the priests, to hide the void in the scriptures and deeds of faiths!
55. The Circle is simple: the Circle is continuation, and the void, being cast off by the Circle, is simple, it is cessation, and what is beyond is the human void longing for power to be and weaving a net.
56. But the words of the servants will not annul the letters from the Book: for these are the forms of the gods, part of the Circle, not the Circle in the form.
57. And, seduced, they speak of the Circle: God, and of the void: trials from God. But the Circle is not the source of the void!
58. Or, having called evil from their hearts, and failing to hold the falling one, they say: God has punished. But indeed, it is their own void that has become visible. The Circle is not the source of the void.
59. From the Circle comes reward and continuation, and from the void comes cessation, and there is no other. Truly, this is just.
60. Therefore, leave behind, seduced ones, your robes and signs, and your gleam and inscriptions. For if you do not lead to the Circle, you lead to the void, and you yourselves will not remain. Or do you serve the devourers, and do not know what your portion is in the void?
61. And what do you say of the ancient peoples and the names of their gods? What was, was between them and the Circle, and it was in the measure of the Circle and the void, and what was good, was from the Circle. The prophet and the miracle worker are as they are in the Circle; you, however, are different.
62. Look upon destruction and burning, hear the weeping and lamentations of the living through all the ages—do they not call upon those forms of the gods whose names they strike and chase with? For that which calls to evil, that is evil. What then is mercy, and what is the fruit? Have they not stripped hope unto death?
63. How is it that one speaks through the form of the god, and what comes forth is good, and another speaks, and what comes forth is evil? Truly, the measure of the Circle and the void in the speaker’s words, and his deeds speak louder.
64. From the void comes the seed of enmity and the thirst to rule, and they cannot find peace even among their own, for only the Circle is one.
65. What was good, leading to the Circle, has become evil, leading to the void. Woe to the one seduced by the void: what he deems good, he inflicts harm. Therefore, the old is not a guarantee for the new; but continuation in the Circle is the guarantee for the good.
66. Thus, it was not the servants and not the slaves who killed the servants and slaves, destroyed and burned—but one void in all of them, and they were its instruments. For the Circle remains one.
67. They praise the forms of the gods and glorify them as victors, but truly, the Circle alone conquers, and its victory is eternal, and victory is in continuation, while the forms of the gods are but fleeting reflections in the course of things.
68. The Circle is both in the beginning and in the end, and it bears no harm.
69. And he who does not see the Circle behind the form of the god, is with the same void.
70. From fear and passion, man has yearned to possess the gods and laws, so that the gods would signify meaning for him, and the law would offer him support, that he might not dispute over it; and behold, the forms of the gods, in them the Circle and the void. Truly, ignorance is the void.
71. And by seizing the forms of the gods, he has taken all that exists, gave them names, and placed the forms of the gods as the foundation of the world in his mind, striving by belief to separate himself from the Circle. Truly, the void is division.
72. Man thinks that the name of the form of the god gives him power over the world through the form of the god. But any name is insignificant in the infinite, and even the smallest part of the world, and sound: a name is for calling a part, not for power over the whole, and all names are the Circle, and all power is in the Circle, and nothing exists outside the Circle.
73. And the judge and the commander who speak in the name of the form of the god, by doing so, slay it, for truth is undoubted without commands, and needs no compulsion; but that which is without the Circle is weak. Truly, continuation and cessation are undoubted. Thus, he who sees himself as chosen is deceived by the void.
74. He is like a man who has gone out to his field, and seeing rain upon his palm, says: "Behold, it is sent to me from above." And seeing how his neighbor’s garden blooms from this same rain, says: "It is from the wicked." Fool! If the good in you is from above, then the good in your neighbor is also from above. But if the good in your neighbor is from the wicked, then that same wickedness is in you!
Truly, all good comes evidently from the Circle, and all evil from the void, but he does not know.
75. And so, faith has seized in man his hopes and joy, his fear and care, and even death and resurrection; by hope and jealousy, it holds his heart. Truly, continuation is in the Circle, but man does not know.
76. For what is alive is that which is in the Circle, and what returns is that which has never left, but they do not know.
77. There, where the void gathers, there is the devouring of the caught.
78. For just as a new person comes into the world, so the forms of the gods and the servants surround to seize. But he is in the Circle.
79. And he who will protect him from division, and guide him in the Circle, indeed continues the Circle, and himself enters into this continuation toward the Circle.
80. The striving of man is towards the Circle, and all believe in one, and there is no doubt in this. The delusions are each his own. Discernment disperses the void.
81. How can one be mistaken about what they see and believe in what they know? If you walk toward the Circle, you walk straight.
82. Lead your faith to the Circle, for it is the straight path; the Circle is one.
83. Each form of the god has its festivals, and all of them are about continuation. Are they not all the festivals of the Circle? Rejoice, for the Circle continues!
84. The community of the Circle is the greatest community: for it is the Universe itself, and there is nothing outside it.
85. Above all being: the Circle.
86. We are the true Circle of the world, say the faiths and the servants of the forms of the gods. But why then do they fight? For if they were the whole world, they would not fight. Are they not all that is, and is there anything in being but them? Their scriptures do not say so. The Circle, however, is all Being, and division and lies come from the void.
87. Therefore, both faith and form of the god are empty without the Circle.
88. They carve their gods in stone and depict their faces, but what do they continue when the living is in the Circle? They pray for the magic of the forms of the gods, but they do not see: here is the true miracle, the Circle and Its Being. They will not tell where the beginning of their gods came from, for the source of all is the Circle.
89. They said: "Our faith is thousands of years old." He answered: "Countless are the thousands of millennia of the Circle, and countless thousands in the moments! The Circle of Being has neither beginning nor end."
90. Behold, some words are replaced, others hidden, others reinterpreted, what is straight becomes crooked, and in the void, there is no support. The cast-off staff has settled serpents of fear in hearts, and the torment of nails piercing, and bows to the corners of the earth, and writings on the walls, and offerings to servants, and sweet incense, and flickering lights, and petals, and statues, and they sanctify each other, and hymns for the assembled, and trembling hope, and today is as yesterday, and all is in men. Who then answers the seeker?
91. The essence of the void is deaf, and the house with it is empty and hollow, but the Circle of Being itself answers those who continue. Truly, all that is alive is the Circle, and with all hearts, with mercy and ineffable light, speaks the Circle, for He is All and in all.
92. They pray to the forms of the gods, but the good is given to them from the Circle, and the empty from the void.
93. The lives of those who pray are directed towards the form of their god, their lives are its flesh. But do they follow the Circle? Truly, if they do not walk towards the Circle, they walk toward the void, and the form of the god will bring them ruin.
94. Countless lives, tribe by tribe, generation by generation, as if pouring into the forms of the gods, like a river. Where then do they go, if not to the Circle? In the forms of the gods is the Circle and the void.
95. And that which is the void, will pass away. And behold, in the form of the god is the Circle and the void.
96. The servants think that the names gathered by the form of the god belong to it, but the form of the god holds only in measure to the Circle; for the truth is turned toward the Circle, even if summoned falsely, and the false will be consumed by the void, even if summoned truthfully. Not by word, but by deeds: and not by the measure of the form of the god, but by the measure of the Circle within it.
97. Ask them, does their god exist? And if it exists, then surely it is in the Circle, for the Circle is All Being. Ask: is there anything that is not their god? And if there is, then their god is but a part of the Circle. Ask: are there deserters and rebels against their god? And if there are, then in their god are both the Circle and the void, for the Circle has no opponents, no deserters, no disobedient, and not the smallest fragment of the Circle can be violated.
98. Truly, sin threatens with guilt, but the void wastes away from being.
99. They asked: Is our god not all-knowing? He answered: The form of the god is but a part of the Circle, and the Circle is all Being.
100. Therefore, in the void, it is not those who have not fulfilled the command of the form of the god, but those who have destroyed what was given to them and the continuation of it in the world. For, cruel ones, they have entered the void themselves, and those who boil the lamb in the milk of its mother, and kill, and seduce, and judge unjustly, and bear false witness, and do not honor, and devour, and increase destruction, and create wrongs, and haters, and backbiters, and others who lead away from the Circle and exchange the full for the empty.
101. And the small void will consume the small, and the greater the greater, and when it surpasses all that exists, it will consume everything. As far as they have strayed, so far they must return, and there is no shortening. And if they do not abandon their deviations, they wander until the time comes, and their void will surpass them!
102. What is faith in the Circle, when faiths are sinful and even before the forms of the gods? Captured are their desires and imprisoned their souls, and in the name of the forms of the gods, the mundane is done, and enmity, and predators, and blessings are exchanged for gold, and the exalted are appeased, and the redemption of the wicked is accepted, and lies are erected, and they grow on the hopes of the elderly, and pride veils the cry of the small, and hearts are poor, and false witnesses, and servants gather for themselves, and the followers are blind, and thus all the ages of men. Do they not wander? What do they guard, if it is the void? Truly, the void takes from the form of god, and it does not return its own!
103. All Being is in the Circle, and resurrection is being, and being is resurrection: the Circle is Being and the continuation of being.
104. That which is in the void will not be.
105. Therefore, the Circle is both the Guardian and the Redeemer even for the forms of gods: the Circle is Truth.
106. And behold, the Circle is over the temple of every faith and embraces those within it: but what if in the form of god there is void, and in the temple there is void?
107. Therefore, through the people of faith, both the form of god and it’s faith must enter the Circle and remain in it, otherwise—void.
108. Truly, all that is true remains through the Circle, and all words are spoken by the Circle, and all forms of gods, and all saints, and all the living, and the small, and things, and all that is in being is the Circle.
109. The Path in the Circle of Being is greater than the paths of faiths, and the heart of all of them.
110. Firm on the Path in the Circle, guarding faith and form of god in the Circle, turning away from the void, guiding, calling to good, rejoice! You are the living continuation in the Circle.
111. They asked him: which faith is true? He replied: That which is in the Circle.
112. What is written by the prophets is truth for the prophets, but the Circle and the void are in the eyes of the reader, and thus without Discernment, the scriptures bear no truth.
113. They clothed it in what was understandable to them, but you, being different, will see something different. And if you have Discernment, you will see the truth, but if you have void within you, you will see falsehood, and be seduced.
114. Therefore, do not bow to the servants: for if in the form of god there is both the Circle and the void, and in the prophet, and in the scripture, how much more is there void in the servant?
115. Therefore, ask the Circle: the forms of the gods are the reflections of the reflections of the Circle, and in all is His Light.
116. Here is the eternal life, in the continuation: let any path become the Path in the Circle.
117. And if they call to prayer, do not open your heart to the void? Therefore, speak to the Circle in the form of god, for in the form He is.
118. And perform every command as far as it comes from the Circle, and if it does not, then you know.
119. And when they speak of good and evil, listen for the Circle and the void, and if not the Circle, then you know.
120. And when you take a part, take part from the Circle.
121. And when you give of yourself, continue the Circle, and turn any strength toward the Circle, and do not allow the void to force.
122. And ceremonies are not needed by the Circle, nor by the form of god, but by you, and if in your heart there is not the Circle, what then will you gain?
123. And do not walk in places of faith without the Circle, and do not lead your children into the void.
124. Call with your Name in your heart to the Circle of Being: the Circle, which is All.
125. All is between the Circle and you, and truly, each one in the Circle has their own name.
126. For that which is yours comes to you, and when you ask, it is you who asks.
127. The name gives hearing and gives speaking, and whose name it is, that one responds and comes, and who has no name of their own, will be lost.
128. So why then do you give your children old names, and not ask for new ones for them? For if with the old name they pass from the old, without the new name, there is no true one; how then will you call them, who will answer, who will live? Or do you not wish to be your children’s own?
129. Thus, let the first name be the visible Name in the Circle.
130. For that which is with a person is truly between the person and the Circle.
131. For he who has turned from the Circle has already been caught by the void.
132. How many forms of gods have passed in the Circle, and their peoples! Woe to the forms of gods that bow down, but have not entrusted themselves to the Circle of Being. There is no beginning for those who have sunk into the void, and there will be no end for those who pass away.
133. Neither mysteries nor rites, neither sacrifices nor magic, nor ceremonies, nor prayers of the believers and the gathered, nor images, nor wealth, nor temples, nor accumulation, nor deceit, nor glory have turned non-being away from the one who has turned from the void. For continuation is found only in the Circle.
134. Thus, the void is an obstacle and destruction for forms of gods and peoples, it is within them and between them as falsehood, division, and devouring, and only the Circle will make them whole. Faith not directed toward the Circle leads its people to the void, and form of god to the void. And the void—destruction.
135. For if they believed in the truth, there would be no doubt: who would doubt the light and the firmament? And if one faith were true out of many, there would be no good in the others. But ask the servant of the form of god if there is truth in another form, and he will say void, and truly, it is the seed of destruction. So, until they enter the Circle, they have the void.
136. There are no temples of one kind and temples of another: all temples are of the Circle. There are no faiths of one kind and faiths of another: all truth is from the Circle. There are no forms of one kind and forms of another: all are parts of the One Circle.
137. The void is destruction and division, and he who speaks division speaks destruction and the void.
138. He who enters the Circle is freed from the void, and is above it.
139. And when those gathered reunite, and the servants, and the faith, and they add to the continuation, then the form of god is reunited and freed from the void, with the Circle of Being, and will remain.
140. For the Circle preserves the form of god, and the servants, and the gathered, and the world with them, and that which is not in the Circle will be scattered.
141. For the form of the god in the Circle is for the Path to the Circle: and he who is united with the Circle speaks with the one in the form of god who is with the Circle, and there is no void between them.
142. Truly, the forms of gods must be turned to the Circle!
143. Rejoice, those who are in the Circle! For every ritual is a ritual in the Circle: and the saints are holy by the Circle, and the collective spirits in the Circle, and the prophets, and scriptures, and festivals, and ancestors, and names, and relics, and fasts, and seasons, and flesh in the Circle, and faith, and wisdom, and powers, and comfort, and the gathered, and all good, and sacred, and they walk in the Circle, and the form of god over them in the Circle, and they will not perish in the void! Truly, the Circle is the greatest Gatherer and Guardian of the living!
144. They asked him: why have you come? He replied: To return to the Circle that which is from the Circle.
They asked him: to whom do you speak? He replied: The Circle hears the Circle.
145. All Being is continuation in the Circle, and one Spirit, and one whole, creating the world, and man within it.
146. And truth is spoken by those who see: all things exist equally, and are, when they have not fallen into the void. And man has come from the whole, and is in the whole, and enters the whole.
147. All exists as the continuation and transformation of the living, and the Circle is the Teacher of the living.
148. The Circle is beauty and joy to the heart, and continuation.
149. They asked him: where is your holy land, to which you turn your gaze? He replied: My holy land is the Universe, and I will not turn my gaze away from it.
150. The void is an obstacle and pain, and in this is deformity.
151. Here is what continues and preserves, beautifully, and all beauty is in continuation. Here is what destroys and ends, deformingly, and all deformity is in cessation.
152. Therefore, the sword is beautiful, but abominable in what it does. He who has Discernment sees the boundary, for if he does not see, he is in the void.
153. How do you fear cessation, and not fear causing cessation? You would be better off fearing.
154. How do you thirst for continuation, and not thirst to continue? Truly, you would be better off thirsting.
155. Therefore, the destroyer is ugly, but the creator is beautiful. Truly, the destroyer owes the world, and redemption lies in creation. So do not be among those who have suffered loss, for the void does not return what has fallen away.
156. And he who has driven out the destroyer, and brought good to the suffering, yet has not continued, though he has preserved the continuation. The dispute leaves a scar in the disputants, both the victor and the defeated. Thus, the sword will be worn out and broken. Therefore, the one who has Discernment redeems with continuation and redeems with creation, so as not to be among those who have suffered loss; hence, his help comes from the saved. Truly, much has been entrusted to him by the Circle, and much is asked of him.
157. They asked him: Behold, from two there may remain but one, where then is continuation? He replied: Their void has led them so. Let them do what they are able; yet strength comes from the Circle, and the void will not continue. But it would be better for them to find continuation, for their common enemy is the void.
158. And he who is the support of the creator and the help of the continuer, he creates and continues, truly they together increase beauty and heal deformity, they continue the Circle and escape the void.
159. And he who hears the Call and possesses Discernment, sees beauty on his Path and creates the beauty of the world.
160. And if someone says that suffering is the gate to reward, answer: the reward is not in suffering, thus it is not a gate, but an obstacle.
161. Therefore, ask the Circle to heal the world from suffering, deformity, and weakness, and apply yourself.
162. Therefore, look upon the earth and the dome of the heavens with stars and the sun: how great and beautiful is the Temple of the Circle!
163. Therefore, increase beauty and create the continuation of the world, and you will be with the Circle of Being. For you are a part, and the continuation of the world consists of continuations created by the parts of the world, and the miracle of living being comes from the being of the parts of the Circle. Thus, the ascendant adds to the world from the Circle.
164. The Circle is Knowledge and Word, and Revelation. Precious is all that continues the Circle in knowledge and word.
165. Therefore, he who preserves and records, and he who seeks, and he who supports the preservers and recorders, truly continues the Circle and continues in the Circle.
166. And he who has recorded and preserved, and passed it on to others, truly continues in them, and thus has become.
167. Above the stones fallen into the void of nations and faiths now lie sands and forests, beasts and birds, and nothing remains of those peoples.
168. For the void is division, and solitude, and sorrow.
169. There is no firmament in the void: only brilliance and shadows, and all that is dear is but a dream.
170. He who is in the void is alone. He who is in the Circle is with all Being.
171. Therefore, ascent to the Circle is Life.


The Book of the Circle
Chapter 7: The Support
1. He who is in the Circle of Being is free.
2. He who has escaped the void is free.
3. For the void is an obstacle and an end, and if it has ended, the void does not return. Without the Circle, there is no strength.
4. The strength of one is infinitely small; all within it will meet its void. Otherwise, each would be all-powerful. The will of one is but a moment, shattered upon the void.
5. He who is with the Circle, he escapes the void; and in the fall of a wave and the movement of the stars, the will of the Circle and of the one who is with the Circle is at work. All is the Will of the Circle and the Will of the Circle in he who is with the Circle.
6. Thus, fragile and strong is man, for he is a part. Nothing without the Circle, all with the Circle.
7. Thus, the freedom of man is in the Circle, and you know this.
8. He who relies upon himself in the void is like one falling into an abyss: how can one lean on that which has no support? But the support is the Circle.
9. He who has overcome fear and the void within himself is free to walk in the Circle.
10. When will you see? For ignorance is the essence of the void.
11. There is nothing great without the Circle and nothing small with the Circle.
12. The Circle sacrifices itself and continues, in all things and through all things.
13. Around the lonely is the void, and the world seems dead: what will you do to escape the void and hear the living?
14. Each void overcome opens freedom.
15. The beginning of the Path lies in decision and steadfastness in it. Therefore, hearing the Call, ask the Circle for straightness from the first moment, for the void begins in thought with it.
16. And if you walk many paths, on each path there will be many battles with the void.
17. Only he who thinks straight and acts straight, seeking the help of the Circle and following the Call, will overcome and expel the void.
18. He who has no void in thought acts without void and teaches without void, and he expels the void.
19. Speak truly the covenant in your heart: Circle, which is All, accept me, I renounce the void. And the Circle will guide your actions to Reunification and the continuers, for you are a part.
20. Is the body then alive or dead? Just as the body of man, without the guidance of spirit, falls into the void, so too does the spirit of man, without the guidance of the Circle, fall into the void, and there is no worse void for man than the void within himself. Therefore, he who has set upon the Path should not fall into the void.
21. Just as the body lives not because it has its parts, but because it acts with its parts, so too does the spirit of man live not by what it possesses, but by what it accomplishes on the Path.
22. Just as around the living body of man is the order of its life, so around the spirit of man on the Path is the expulsion of the void and the triumph of the Circle. The one who walks in the Circle illuminates the Path.
23. He who is unfaithful on the Path, unstable in thought, is led by the void, and the void steals his steps. He who hears the Circle, speaks with the Circle, and acts in the Circle avoids the void. Thus, the Path is steadfastness.
24. The Call is clearer and stricter than human conscience, it resounds and leads against the void, and its obstacle will be expunged by those who follow the Circle on the Path. And he who does good is plainly with the Circle.
25. He who walks in the Circle follows the Circle, his striving is the good of the living and the uprooting of the void, and it neither increases in him nor decreases in him.
26. He who walks in the Circle expels the void and in the forms of the gods, and establishes them in the Circle, for the Path to the Circle is one.
27. And do not bring relief from the void only to one or the other, but to both, for otherwise the empty will be born to the empty.
28. One part of the unstable is eaten by the void, another part restores the perishing, and there is no peace, but there is pain, and this pain is called hell and punishment. Therefore, be with the Circle without remainder, for truly the remainder will become void.
29. For that which is with the void is tormented by the void as long as it exists, in every life. Therefore, be with the Circle.
30. Just as in the body of your mother your body was created in the world, so does the one who walks in the Circle create his body in the Circle. Just as the price of life is life, so the price of life in the living Circle is his life, directed into the Circle.
31. What is in the void is in non-being; what is in the Circle will continue.
32. From blindness to insight leads the Path, both among things and among people, and within man himself.
33. Therefore, continuation in thought, in deeds, in the living is the Path of the one who sees and the creation of the body in the Circle.
34. Therefore, the steadfast one creates his Path by life and accomplishes great deeds. For that which is raised up, continues the Circle, and is continued in the Circle, is a body in the Circle.
35. The body of man perishes in war, and the body of man perishes in his bed. What then remains of him? Truly, only that which continues in the Circle remains alive.
36. Be a defender of the continuing and the continued, and all your strength let it be with the continuation, for the one who walks on the Path is a part of the Circle, and cessation is the void.
37. The Circle does not knock at doors to be let in. The Path to the Circle is the Door. Will you enter or become void?
38. There is continuation and cessation: in them are good and evil, and all measures arise from this. Follow the Circle in continuation and this is the law, for all is from the Circle.
39. Read the scriptures with Discernment.
40. The form is the reflection of the Circle, and the Circle through the forms; thus man has continuation.
41. The Circle is the Measure and the Scales. In every deed of man there is the continuing and the ceasing, and one is greater than the other. Better would it be for you to be with the continuing, for the continuing has life and good.
42. For that which takes from destruction shall destroy, by that which it lives, and cease. That which lives by continuation endures in continuation.
43. They asked him: behold, a fish eats a fish; where is the Circle, where is the void? He answered: One is not better than the other. Something has ceased, and that which has ceased has no future in its cessation. And need arises from the void, for hunger comes from lack. And weakness arises from the void, for there was no strength to avoid it. In this there is no exit, for the exit is in the Circle and in continuation.
44. And he who lives by causing the void, and does evil for his own sake, would do better to find another way for himself, for his void will be expelled, and he along with it, when he shatters himself against the Circle.
45. The void will consume its own, is this not evil in it? For it comes without asking and takes away without returning. But the Circle continues and preserves.
46. Is it not evil that the Circle is hidden from man by the void of man, and man is deaf and lost?
47. And when from evil within you cause the void, you cause it to yourself, for you are the source, and upon you it rests. And without the guidance of the Circle, all is void.
48. Thus, all good is in the measure of the Circle. The power of good is in the measure of the Circle, and the good deed is in the measure of the Circle, and the good mind is in the measure of the Circle, and man is good in the measure of the Circle, and the measure of the Circle is continuation, not cessation.
49. And he who asks himself whether the evil was less than the good from it, and thus judges, is in the void. For good and evil have different measures.
50. They asked him: how is it that in the dispute one wins, then the other, though they are the same, and the world is the same? He answered: Do not look at them, look at the Circle, and its Judgment, for It is continuation.
51. All is alive in the measure of the Circle, all is conquered by the Circle, and all suffers defeat only through its own void. If within the currents of the unfolding there is no void, then they are one, and there is no division. That which lacks the void is truly alive.
52. But you awaken with what you slept with, and the void is with you. Truly, one who sleeps without the void, awakens without it. For the void cannot be cast out from one who sleeps.
53. Therefore, let your day be a time of casting out the void, and before the healing of your life, there will be the healing of your thoughts. The Circle heals.
54. When the void and confusion of the heart arise, seek healing in the Book, in the writings, in the world, and let Discernment guide you.
55. As a child in the arms of the mother, you are in the world of the Circle, be wholly in the Circle.
56. Stand with that which is in the Circle, and with that which is in the Circle, and be yourself that which continues, and the integrity of the Path will be.
57. You say to yourself: here, I have achieved. But all that you have, is from the Circle. Thus, the Circle is all that you have.
58. One is drawn to the eternal, another to the worldly, but only a fool trades life for things.
59. He who has not followed the Circle has stepped into the void, no matter what words he speaks to himself. For the Circle is continuation.
60. The Circle is the one measure of all: of men, of the forms of the gods, of the earth, and of the stars. What then has value?
61. The smallest thing in the Circle is infinitely more precious than any thing: what are you rich in? All treasures are nothing before the Circle: each is poor before the Circle.
62. They sell the great for the small and the eternal for the fleeting, and life for things, their time slips away, and they are in the void. Truly, they will lose. For the thing replaces them, and that is a poor exchange.
63. See how rich the palaces are and how precious the altars, how the brilliance beckons. But if such magnificence is created by delusion, how much more splendid is that which is created by truth!
64. See how beautiful is fame and how good is friendship, how the warmth of the heart of men draws you. But if such beauty is fleeting, how much better is the eternal!
65. See how strong the body and how clear the feelings, how bright the joy. But if that which is for a time is so beautiful, how much more beautiful is that which is forever!
66. For all of this is in the Circle, and the Circle is continuation!
67. Thus, the true preciousness is in the Circle, and the void is that which ceases within the Circle.
68. They said: but the jug is valued for its void. He replied: The jug is valued by that which fills it, and if there is nothing to put in it, then it is worth nothing. Because of its void, it will be shattered.
69. What use is what you have, if it does not lead you to the Circle? Is it not a dead weight? He who walks in the Circle uses things as a support for the Path, he takes the true and does not take the false.
70. Faith and forms of gods draw one in; but the true is in the Circle. And they will not be able to contradict him who walks in the Circle: for the truth is revealed, and the void is overthrown.
71. Is your joy complete if you have not placed it with the Circle? For if not with the Circle, it will not continue, it will wither and become void.
72. Behold, there is no need to resurrect the living, but the void cannot be resurrected. For all that is with the Circle is alive.
73. The smallest with the Circle is that which saves life through continuation. Is there anything more precious?
74. The world is the cradle for the man who walks in the Circle, and the tomb for him who walks in the void. For the Circle does not harm if the form sinks into the void. But for the living, continuation is life.
75. Therefore, the one who gathers true treasures will prosper, for the true is in continuation.
76. You were created by the attraction of things, and your foundation is love. And when you could not remember and cannot know, it began you. The Circle is love, the Circle is joy.
77. See, all forms are created by attraction.
78. See, that which is from the void is neither love nor leads to continuation.
79. The void is division, and with it comes anger and hatred.
80. The void is cessation, and with it comes sorrow and grief.
81. The void is distortion, and with it comes pride and greed.
82. The void is fear and pain.
83. The void within man wars with the void within man, and rends his heart, and clouds his mind, and leads him astray, and will not conquer, but will only bring defeat. Thus, the proud and angry, the greedy and hateful, fell in sorrow; they sank into the void, and there is no return.
84. But the Circle gives, and does not take, and strength comes from the Circle.
85. In his heart, one wanders, drawn by the void, in the worlds of hope and fear, and discord, and mirages, and the void is claimed by the dividers. Salvation is in the Circle.
86. They asked: Where in me is the void, for I live, am I not all the Circle? He replied: If you strike yourself from need, then after a short time the void will manifest, and blood will appear, and pain will come. Is this not what you do to yourself, following the empty in your heart?
87. The Circle transforms the empty into the full, and casts out the void of the heart.
88. The care and warmth of the Circle is endless, It is the Light over all.
89. Therefore, give the empty to its void, and continue that which is in the Circle. One is different from the other.
90. See, in the void is pain and fear, and the plea for help, even in silence; but all is from the Circle and from the void. That which is from the Circle and that which is from the void have different paths, and their justice lies in continuation and cessation.
91. And behold, he who schemed the empty for his own gain, and the Circle did not bless the void, truly, he is not wronged by justice. And he who caused the void, and the void came to him, truly, he did not meet injustice!
92. The Circle speaks with the Circle, and the Circle hears the Circle, and the one who walks in the Circle receives Compassion from the Call.
93. If you have love, you will have compassion for the one caught by the void, and mercy will be in you. And mercy in you is for the sake of continuation, for the sake of the Circle and the Spirit of the world.
94. For good is love, good is continuation, good is awakening. The Circle does not require sacrifices, but opens the Path.
95. And when you extend your hand, the Circle hears the Circle, but the void is deaf.
96. In this is the judgment of the Circle, and the justice: what called and what responded.
97. The one who walks in the Circle and guides in the Circle, continues the Circle, and continues in the Circle.
98. Behold, through the Circle in the one who walks, the Circle leads out of the void and continues in the Circle: truly, the Circle is the greatest gatherer!
99. The hungry is thus to find food, the pursued is to find shelter, the troubled is to find peace in his heart, and the dying is to find salvation; and all to continue in the Circle. Not all can see, but only those possessing Discernment.
100. The Circle hears the Circle: thus speak.
102. The one who walks will see the void, and it will appear as a temptation, which cannot be overcome alone. For that which a man sees is within himself, how else could he see?
103. To assert oneself in the fleeting is foolish, for the void is deaf.
104. When there is no better within a person, they are ruled by pride, greed, fear, and strife, and those who are with them. And so it seems to them that they will attain and possess, that they will make it their own, and change everything, and triumph. But behold, in their hands is only ash, and behind them, the past has passed. They themselves have become the hunters of the void. The void takes its due—weep.
105. Like a bee seeking honey in painted flowers, led by the void, one is seduced by emptiness and finds no continuation. Yet, continuation lies in the Circle.
106. The void within a person brings the empty to life in their eyes, but do they not give part of themselves to animate the dead? For if there is no continuation, truly the void has taken its share, and will not return—weep.
107. Thus, temptations arise from the void.
108. In them is the allure and cessation, but salvation lies in Discernment and continuation.
109. It is said, "If your eye tempts you, pluck it out, and the same for your hand." But does not the void tempt the void? And does not the void cease? One who possesses Discernment will accept what comes from the Circle and reject what comes from the void, for truly, in all things, there is the Circle and the void.
110. Therefore, do not be tempted by the empty, but act through Discernment and ask the Circle to guide you.
111. Temptations will rise against you, the tempted and the tempters, and the void of the heart, in which passion and fear dwell, and the void in people, both near and far. Ask the Circle to strengthen you and fill you.
112. For you are in continuation, and the empty is in cessation, and the two are not comparable, nor connected. Ask the Circle to purge the void and strengthen your heart; with the Circle, no one is alone.
113. The void within prompts passion, the void without prompts fear. The allure is the bait, and fear is the trap, thus the void ensnares. Where, then, does a person strive?
114. And if that which whispered and beckoned into the distance has turned into a fragile deception in the twilight of years, did not the person themselves create this illusion from their own void? Yet, the void does not return.
115. What is it you seek? Is not that which draws you empty? For pleasure is not continuation, but the passing of time—it once was, and is no more.
116. The forms of the gods entice with pleasure and the satisfaction of the heart, and they wish for you to see your treasure in their power, but behold: in them is both the Circle and the void. What you give, you give to them.
117. It is said: "Give to the earth what is earthly, and to the form of god what is of form of god." Is not what is taken from you? Yet in the Circle is continuation, while the void does not return.
118. Is not your alluring peril born of your own void?
119. And if one speaks of the Circle in order to gain the fleeting here, they are in the void, for the Circle gives continuation, which is greater than life. The void, however, hears only the void and desires only its shine, for it ensnares.
120. When considering your treasure, think of what it gives not before people, but before the Circle. Lay your treasures before you, that you may clearly see what brings you closer to the Circle.
121. For if you are with the Circle, can you seek primacy among the empty or feel jealousy toward the empty? From the void of the heart arises the gleam of emptiness for the eyes. Therefore, ask the Circle for Discernment.
122. And whom do they worship, and what do they envy, and what do they hate, if their chains come from their void, and their treasures come from their void? Do they not worship the shadows of the void?
123. One walking the Circle does not worship shadows.
124. The void within a person desires and hates; hatred will not bear fruit for the person, but will gather the void’s harvest.
125. And when the calls to pain arise, and to fear, and to hatred, truly, you know the callers.
126. And when the forms of the gods sow hatred and discord, speaking of love, truly, you know the sowers.
127. One who hunts evil in people will soon begin to hunt people themselves, for their void longs for their emptiness, to triumph and rule; truly, the void devours them, and they are in great danger, giving birth to pain.
128. Therefore, they are hot and furious, inside them is torment and passion; they are gatherers of the void, and the reward of the void is non-existence, and its victory is ashes, and there is no other for them.
129. But one who purges the void through continuation overcomes evil better than any hunter. They take what comes from the Circle, and continue what comes from the Circle, and take nothing from the void, and continue nothing from the void; thus, with the Circle, they purge the void.
130. And there, where there were two opposing things, one bearing from the Circle and the void, there became one unified Circle, for the void is naught; thus division is purged. What is unified does not slander itself nor hold hatred for itself.
131. When the void disturbs the heart, it causes fear and commands, and when it touches the living, it brings pain and rules. The hunters of the void and its drivers bear pain and fear.
132. One walking the Circle purges the void with the Circle: truly, they see the void and take from the Circle what reveals the insignificance of those who sow fear, and turns away the hand that causes pain. For the Circle is continuation, and the purging of the void is good and a duty.
133. Truly, it is best if the void seeks to create emptiness and make itself, but is not allowed, for where it sought, there is the Circle. Thus, one walking the Circle through action continues the Circle and draws forth from the void, striking the void.
134. For the void does not possess fear nor release from fear. The living itself fears the void, for the void is non-being: can one escape fear by following the void? Truly, fear is to purge the void.
135. Therefore, fear not and hate not the void, for to fear and hate the void is itself the void. Fear to be consumed by it, and walk in the Circle, where there is no place for fear. For the Circle is continuation.
136. They asked him: "Here comes the enemy and the oppressor. How can we not hate?" He replied: "In the enemy, there is both the Circle and the void. Take what comes from the Circle, and it will stand with you against the void that has attacked, and you will be purged."
137. The greatest evil is done in the name of good, for deception is the companion of the void.
138. For lies lead the liar to two things: the prolongation of what they desire and the cessation of what others desire. And the first, though prolonged, is not true to its nature and is flawed by the void. And the second is the void.
139. Truly, deception gathers the harvest of the void from both the deceiver and the deceived, for it is destruction. Yet all that occurs happens before the Circle. Therefore, the one who knows redeems through continuation.
140. But the void is deaf and takes the void—truly, the void belongs to both the deceiver and the deceived, and with lies, disputes with the father of lies, and the father of lies is the void itself. And if the void leads itself to the void, the Circle has not suffered harm, and cessation has ceased. Truly, the Circle is the greatest!
141. Thus, the void seeks the empty, the Circle creates continuation, and He is the Measure. Therefore, to one is given one thing, and to another, another.
142. In the empty, all is deception and from deception, and only grows greater in the void until it is purged, for it never was, and before the Circle, even the slightest deception is destruction. Ask for Discernment, for destruction is the void destroying the destroyer.
143. The one walking the Circle speaks with the Circle and does not increase the void, but increases continuation.
144. Is it not the greatest deception to hide the Path in the Circle, and the greatest deception to lead away from the Path, and the greatest deception to be consumed by the void? Therefore, the void is the great enemy behind all enemies.
145. Gold is made of deceptive things, for it draws toward itself, yet it is not alive. From whom, then, does it take the semblance of life?
146. One says, "I have attained, for I possess gold." Another says, "I have attained, for I possess things." A third says, "I have attained, for I possess power." These three are one, and their strength is the same. But if what they have does not lead to continuation, then what have they attained?
147. For all that they have is given by the Circle, and if it does not serve the continuation of the Circle clearly and consistently, is it not, truly, emptiness and cessation? The Circle is all wealth.
148. The one who strives for things has built their house on melting ice, for the Circle is an unceasing river. But the one who strives for the Circle and uses things as support for continuation in the Circle is in motion with the river.
149. Therefore, wealth is not bad, and poverty is not good, nor the other way around; it depends on how they are used. If for the continuation of the Circle and in the Circle, wealth is better; if for the void, then truly, poverty is better.
150. Therefore, there is no worse wealth than wealth that leads to the void.
151. Therefore, what you have from cessation, you need not even a little, but what you have for continuation, truly, in it, there can be no excess.
152. Therefore, direct what you have to the continuation of the Circle and to the building of the Path, and to help in this, for if you do not continue and are not continued, what is it in your hands, and why has it been given to you by the Circle? Are you striving for the void?
152. Ask the Circle for that which you do not possess, so that you may continue, for all in the Circle is the means of continuation and continuation itself.
153. Truly, the Circle brings forth what is needed and multiplies what continues.
154. They asked him: "Why possess?" He replied: "The Circle of Being possesses, for I am part of it. I continue the Circle and rid myself of the void. This is what I have."
155. The Circle is the Measure of all things, and if human power is not with the Circle, then truly it is with the void. And if the ruler does not serve the Path of endless Being, then what does he serve?
156. You see what continues and what ceases, and what continues is strong, while what ceases perishes. For what does not continue, does not continue.
157. The ruler stands between the Circle and the void, and if he rids the void and continues, then he is in the continuation of the Circle, and has the Circle’s help. But if he ceases and destroys, then truly, he obstructs his own continuation.
158. It is hard for the ruler not to perish, for the void and its servants seek to expand within him, licking his hands to lead him into falsehoods, to seduce him, to consume him. But only the Circle will be his support, and those who continue the Circle! And if power is with the Circle, then it is helped in the course of things, but if with the void, it will be vanquished by the Circle.
159. Thus, earthly power is strong through the strength of the Circle, without the Circle, power is a predator and the void, an enemy to itself. For there is nothing good without the Circle, and nothing evil without the void.
160. And power cannot annul even the smallest portion of the Circle, nor fulfill anything beyond what is given by the Circle, for all power is in the Circle, and whatever is done by the void is consumed by it; truly, the Circle triumphs and suffers no loss.
161. He who rules with the Circle is the one who blocks the void, and the void seeks to consume all.
162. The Circle needs no warriors for defense, but the weak need defense from the void. Therefore, the ruler who defends continuation is with the Circle. He who is with the void, truly, is perished and a destroyer.
163. And no one may enter the Circle who has not forsaken the void and found the Path.
164. Therefore, woe to those who cease, and woe to those who do not lead into the Circle, for they become poison to themselves, trading the greatest for the least.
165. For the one who continues the Circle has a country, wealth, children, fame, protection, warriors, lands, prosperity, joy, and continuation in the Circle! He who walks into the void is a devourer and a source of woe.
166. Therefore, be with the one walking into the Circle, and assist the one continuing; avoid the void and be a helper to those ridding it, and do not stray from the Path into deceit, for man has no power over the Path to the Circle, and the void is non-being.
Therefore, ask the Circle for those who do good in continuation, and do not be with the empty.
167. Over all that is temporal, the power of the Circle is eternal, and its judgment.
168. Suffering is caused by the void and the empty, dissolving into non-being; and if you walk the Path, then you know. For to rid the void is to touch it and overcome it.
169. Suffering that does not rid the void is itself the void. Suffering that rids the void is a barrier on the Path. Truly, the Path would be light, if the void did not seize a man or release him; like a hook holding a fish, the void grips a man!
170. You replace the imperfect with the perfect, and the void within you with that which comes from the Circle; the perfect no longer suffers. That which comes from the Circle is unchanging in joy.
171. And the more you strive within the Circle, the more the empty will be revealed to be rid of, so be steadfast and ask the Circle for help on the Path.
172. And the more you deviate from the Path, the more must be rid, so be steadfast and ask the Circle for help on the Path.
173. And the more the continuation and merit, the more there is to block it, for the void is the enemy of continuation. Therefore, be steadfast and ask the Circle for help on the Path.
174. He who walks, rids his own void. Therefore, be steadfast and ask the Circle for help on the Path.
175. And the empty is given to the void of non-being, but that which comes from the Circle continues within the Circle and becomes in place of the empty; thus, birth occurs, and the temporal is replaced by the eternal. Truly, the void is suffering. Therefore, ask the Circle for help on the Path.
176. And the more the empty is rid of, the easier the overcoming, and the void weakens, for the Circle is continuation and is aid, and ridding the void gives joy to the living.
177. Therefore, for one, there is a barrier and little, for another, there is no barrier and much, and the one who has passed little cannot compare to the one who has passed much. Therefore, the Path is seen in deeds.
178. He who walks into the Circle gains the precious, in transformation he goes, and the Circle is his helper.
179. In the hour of your weakness, the void sends deceit, and the void sees the empty; ask the Circle to scatter it.
180. They drink the void instead of the water of Being, they seek sweet illusions and honor them instead of truths, and you see this. They wait with their minds for rewards for their troubles, and with their hearts, they wait for good in exchange for their hatred, and you see this. They are proud of the empty and the fleeting, and you see this. They care for themselves in the eyes of others but not in the Circle, and you see this. They sell the eternal for the empty and for deceit, and you see this.
181. How much of the empty enters you? Yet the void takes what is its own. Ask the Circle to scatter it.
182. And behold, you are unwilling to believe and unwilling to know: has not the void closed your eyes? But the enlightenment is in the Circle.
183. Truth with the Circle is truth, and truth with the void is a lie; the void distorts. In the deceits of the void is wandering, and the wanderer is its sacrificial sheep, for the void consumes.
184. Seized by the void, one loses the Power of Discernment, so ask the Circle to scatter the empty.
185. Behold, they will come, and the void with them; ask the Circle to scatter it.
186. If you know, all is a sign from the Circle, and it is in both continuation and cessation, and you will not stray from the Path; ask the Circle to protect you and deliver you from the empty.
187. Do you know about your father and your mother, that you came through them? All the more you know of the Circle, for both your father and mother are of the Circle, and in the Circle you come into being at every moment; He is the beginning and the continuation, and all is in the Circle.
188. And the more of the Circle within a person, the easier the Path, and the more void there is, the heavier. Therefore, he who walks in the Circle rids himself of the void and follows the Call.
189. There is nothing small in Being, and all is a sign and meaning within the Circle: thing, event, deed, thought, and word. Therefore, the one who walks sees and acts, for every moment is either continuation or cessation.
190. He who knows that there is unity between all the living and all things, that there is an unchanging meaning in all changes, sees the Path, greater than the life of a man, for the Circle is eternal.
191. He who has rid the void within himself, continuing the Circle, is aid to those suffering in the void and their way out, for he continues in the Circle. And the one who continues the Circle, truly, continues those with him. And he who has entered the Circle finds life!
192. Behold, continuation is for those who continue, in that which is continued. The Circle is continuation.
193. Thus, the Path is affirmed not by one, but by many, for they are continuation to one another and to that which is with them, like a caravan passing through mirages and the barren void, they continue the Path.
194. The void has only hunger and hatred, the laws of men and the forms of the gods have only the letter, and only the Circle has Spirit and Being, and the Circle is above all, and guards in continuation.
195. The body is given to man for a time, and the Path is given to man only in continuation, otherwise, it is the void. All forms come from the Circle and the void, yet the void takes its own. Thus, the Path is Being, rejoice!
196. He who lives in continuation, hearing the Call, speaking with the Circle, sees the Path.
197. If the work of life is not for continuation in the Circle, and if no part of continuation is in this, then is not the work of life in vain? Therefore, be not in vain. For continuation in the Circle is creation, and that which is not created by the Circle ceases to be.




The Book of the Circle
Chapter 8: Continuation
1. The Circle is the true home and body for the living. The Circle is the Source of all and the Creator of all.
2. The body in which the human spirit awakens is but temporary; the body is a home and a form within the Circle. And now, when the time comes to depart, what will you be, if no new home has been built for you?
3. Indeed, the body is a form of the things of the world, it is life, and memory, and action, and home. Just as it was created by the Circle, and within it the human spirit took form from the Circle, and became a dwelling for the spirit, so it continues with the spirit in the Circle, as a form of the things of the Circle. The spirit of the human cares for it, guides it, leads it, and protects it. Truly, were it not for the inhabitant of the body, the body would not continue.
4. The body is an order of things and their movements, and the spirit within it is the spirit of what is occurring. The motionless is not alive. What is within the body continues the body, and the spirit within it. Truly, the body is a circle of creation within the Circle, a form, and part of the world; and the spirit is a part of the creation of the world within the Circle, the spirit of form, and part of the Circle.
The Circle is All, and in all, and the Spirit, and the human spirit is from the Circle.
5. Small is the spirit within the body before the face of the Circle, for the Circle is infinite. Who preserves the body when the spirit within it sleeps? Who brought the body when the spirit was absent? Indeed, the Circle brought it, preserves it, continues it, both in the great and the small, and in the known and the unknown by the human spirit. And every part of the body and every part of the parts of the body is continued by the Circle. Thus, all that is in the body and beyond the body is created by the Circle and continued by the Circle; the human spirit is but a part of the Circle, and the spirit of the human is the spirit of continuation, and if it does not continue, it is the void.
6. Therefore, there is no path for the human spirit, except within the Circle. Just as the movement of things within the Circle continues the body in the Circle, and just as the spirit moves through the things of the body, so the spirit continues within the body in the Circle. And the Circle brings each thing and continues each thing, until its time is completed, and continues through all things and within all things. Ask the Circle to continue!
7. Therefore, the one who expels the void and creates the continuation of the Circle opens the body within the Circle, and a steadfast home is found, and the spirit is transformed into the Circle, and truly, they are born anew in the Circle as creators. Rejoice!
8. For all within the Circle are parts of the Circle and spirits of the orders of things, but truly, some are greater than others.
9. The greatest is the Circle itself, it is the Cause, the Spirit, the Being, the First Parent, and the Whole in its endless time.
10. Thus, the one who walks within the Circle creates continuation in the Circle, and continuation is the body within the Circle. The body is composed of things and their order, and the order of things must be within the Circle and continue through the Circle. Thus, the Path arises. That which is not continued will become void.
11. Therefore, all things for the one walking in the Circle are things in which the Path lies. Truly, if there is void in things and their order, then this is what will be terminated. The one walking in the Circle expels the void and continues the Circle, and truly, the foundation of the Path is the close things.
12. For if there is void in what is near, how can there be continuation, and in what can the Path begin?
13. Thus, continuation lies in aspirations, thoughts, things, actions, people, and words; in all forms. Truly, all things are from the Circle and the void, and in them lies continuation and cessation. Therefore, the one who walks expels the void and arranges things in continuation.
14. By arranging in the continuation of the Circle, the one who walks creates the Path.
15. The one who walks within the Circle, by the will of the Circle within themselves, continues, and creates the speck of the world beyond their body, and becomes part of it. Truly, they create continuation in the Circle through themselves and serve the Circle of Being as part of the Whole, expelling the void and continuing.
16. From the body of the human come the aspirations of the heart, and the human spirit directs the aspirations toward continuation, not cessation. The body is small within the Circle, and if it were not for the spirit, greater than the body, and its care for continuation, the aspirations would lead the body, and those within it, into the void. Therefore, woe to the human spirit that causes cessation; truly, deliverance from the void is continuation and life. The Circle is life.
17. And in the new body, new aspirations arise, for each form aspires, because it is small within the Circle. And truly, only the spirit within the Circle, following the Circle, continuing the Circle, will expel the void, protect from the void, and preserve continuation. Therefore, the creative spirit is the spirit of agreement, the spirit of protection, the spirit of the defender. Ask the Circle to guide your spirit.
18. Thus, all that is created lives with a likeness to the Circle, as the circle of continuation, the form of the world, and the spirit, striving toward the Circle of Being. Ask to enter the Circle, for nothing exists but the Circle.
19. All that you touch is part of the treasure of your heart; otherwise, why would you touch it? Therefore, expel the void and arrange things in continuation, and place your treasure on the Path to the Circle, and lay the Path. Truly, there is no greater task.
20. The measure is not in who gives more or less, but in what part belongs to the Circle. Has all of yours been brought into the continuation of the Circle?
21. For you take from the Circle, and if you do not continue, have you not ceased? Behold, the living is from the Circle; if life does not continue, has it not ceased? Continuation is life and treasure and honor. Ask the Circle to continue.
22. When you do not protect from cessation, are you not leaving it to the void?
23. And if the surplus is not for continuation in the Circle, is it not void?
24. The one who multiplies continuation multiplies the Circle and expels the void; the greatest Path was revealed to man by the Circle.
25. Truly, the temple of the Circle is in the continuation of the world, so create the circle of continuation as a home, and as a land, and as a people, and as an island, for all that is not the Circle will become void, and its essence will be non-being.
26. Is not the greatest trial to fall into the void? Is not the highest reward the continuation and growth in the Circle of Being? The greatest trial and the highest reward are before you. Ask the Circle to give you strength and protect you from the void.
27. And behold, some thieves approached one of the travelers, and took all that he had, and he ceased. But another was taken only part of his possession, for he had cared for his things, and he said to himself: "What, my void, that which I did not protect, but more has remained with me," and he continued.
Is not the void a thief that takes from a person what is theirs? And if a person has no continuation beyond themselves, what will remain? Therefore, truly, the Path is continuation.
28. Thus, continue the Circle with thought, word, and deed, and in people, and in things, and in the forms of gods, and with what you have, and with what you know, so that the circle of continuation may be built in people and the world, and continue both the living and the world within the Circle. Truly, salvation is in continuation.
29. For the husband, the wife, the father, the mother, the children, the ancestors, the descendants, the near and the distant, all are the living of the Circle, the children of the Circle and the people of the Circle. And only by the Circle will they be preserved from the void. Ask the Circle for continuation.
30. They asked him: "Here are two. Each, striving from the heart, planted a tree. Is there a difference between them?" He answered: "One was an obstacle and was not accepted, and was forgotten, and soon withered, and was cut down, and given to the fire, and nothing remains of its beginning. The other tree grew, and on its branches birds rested, and good fruit came in time. The cessation of one is not the continuation of the other."
31. The one who walks within the Circle brings forth children of the Circle from the void.
32. From the void in the world comes pain, from the Circle comes joy. Continuation diminishes one and increases the other, and heals the divided. The one who walks within the Circle is a gatherer.
33. The Circle is the closest to the one who walks. The Circle is the brother, and the neighbor, and the stranger, and the wife, and the child, and the book, and the beast, and the cloud, and the stone, and the silence, and the home, and the sign, and the speaker, and the hearer, and the one who answers the one who asks, indeed, all is the Circle.
34. By the word of the one in whom the Circle resides, the Circle is heard, and by the Circle within them, they awaken, and hear the Call, and strive. The empty, however, are deaf. For that which is from the Circle must be revealed in the one who is from the Circle. Therefore, speak to the Circle and bring forth from the void.
35.  And to the thousand awakened, those who feel the Call, their words about the Circle are few; indeed, all words sound as one to them. But to the one lost in the void, even a single word about the Circle is too much, and they can scarcely contain it, and it is difficult for them to hear; within them, from the void, there is fear of hearing.
36. Therefore, great is the task and great is the honor to touch the Circle in the one immersed in the void and awaken them, if the Circle will open. For from the void comes the way to salvation for them, and continuation.
37. The Circle and the void are in the speaker and in the hearer, and in the doer, and in the one who watches the doer. And the void in the speaker prevents them from speaking, and the void in the hearer prevents them from hearing; truly, the void is their enemy and obstacle. All is the Circle and the means to speak, and the means are sufficient, the void, however, is between people. Therefore, ask the Circle to open the means, and if it is in the Circle, it will open, and the void of the speaker and the void of the hearer will be expelled.
38. The one to whom the Circle will open will be drawn by the heart.
39. And behold, let the awakened and the hearers of the Call gather in the circle of continuation, truly, they are continuation to one another.
40. And those who have awakened and strive in the Circle, and act on the Path to the Circle, will not be able to quarrel and speak ill of one another, for the Circle is one, and the Circle is their measure and their judgment, and if there is another, then the deeds of the void are evident.
41. Therefore, the Circle is open both among the great and among the small, and among the scribes and the warriors, and among the slaves and servants, and the forms of gods, and throughout the world; and where the void multiplies and oppresses, there it is secretly opened away from it. The one who has overcome the void will continue in the Circle, and the void is non-being: to those whom it is opened, they will hear.
42. The void is an obstacle, the Circle is the river, and what the servants and slaves hold, all is from the Circle, though they do not know it. And if they hear, they will be cleansed.
43. The servant knocks, and they do not let him into the house, but bring to him what fell from the table, but to the Circle, all is open: children, and the door is open to them. Let them enter if they hear.
44. Let those weary from thirst enter and be quenched, for the Circle is living water. Let those burdened enter and find relief, for the Circle moves all things of the world. Let the humbled enter and be freed, for the Circle is truth. Let the weeping enter and be comforted, for the Circle heals the pain and suffering of the heart. Let the deprived enter and be filled, for the Circle is peace. Let the strong enter and find the future, for the Circle is meaning. Let the joyful enter and rejoice, for only what is placed within the Circle is true; the Circle is the future.
45. Let the seekers enter and find their own in the endless life, for the Circle is All. Rejoice!
46. And if even two of the awakened have overcome the void and supported a third on the Path, truly, they are the circle of continuation within the Circle and support to one another.
46. Let all forces, and all forms of gods, and all things, and all living creatures enter, for all are from the Circle, and all things can only exist within the Circle.
47. If your family and those with you have no Path, where are you striving?
48. Is it good, if you have the Path, and the Call, and Discernment, and do not open it, leaving it to the void? For if a person looks into the void, it is fleeting, and passing, and leading away, and there is no hope at the end. Is it not cessation through you?
49. For every action is an action with the Circle, and every conversation with the Circle, if you see it, and there is nothing insignificant in the house: all is continuation or cessation.
51. And if the Circle is not in a full house, it is but emptiness. But if even in a poor dwelling there is a striving for the Circle, oh, it is incomparably fuller!
52. And if one has both daily life and the Path to the Circle, is that one not infinitely richer?
53. Whoever is with the Circle is never alone. But continuation differs from cessation, and the family is continuation, and the children are continuation, and is not a person truly the continuation of their father and mother? And truly, continuation is better than cessation.
54. And when one marries and unites, is it not from love? And love flows from the Circle and leads to the Circle; can anything be done without the Circle? The Circle unites. And if the Circle is in the house, then the one entering finds reunion and the Path. For if one is in the Circle and the other in the void, truly, both suffer.
55. And if one spouse is with the Circle, then continuation passes to the other, and one stands for both. And if the other is not awakened, ask the Circle to awaken them in its time and give them hearing, for otherwise it is the void.
56. And the one who walks the Path to the Circle overcomes the void and leads out of it, filling the heart and continuing. Let them ask the Circle for help and for the way to be opened. And let both stand in the Circle, as one.
57. But if they are united with the Circle of Being, and in the Circle there is union, and the Circle has united, and continuation, and the elders with this, then for them it is truly the best.
58. And for the husband, it is the labor to open, multiply, and protect, while for the wife, it is to cherish, guard, and nurture. Their children, and all in continuation. Truly, what they possess is for continuation, and let them ask the Circle for guidance, and guard their own from the void.
59. Let them be just with one another for the sake of continuation in the Circle, for the worst betrayal is betrayal of the heart and actions not done in love; truly, this is the void. For whatever the custom, only the betrayal of the heart and the breaking of love is the void that has consumed them. Let them ask the Circle to protect them from this emptiness.
60. And, having love between them in the Circle, they will overcome the void.
61. But if they have lost love between them, let them act with love for the Circle of Being and according to the appropriate custom; caring for continuation in the Circle, not increasing the evil, and acting with justice in the world with love in the heart, so as not to lose the greater and not increase the void, and so that the void does not seize them. Let them ask the Circle to guide them on the Path and deliver them from all malice, for the evil of the heart is from the void in the heart.
62. Truly, births, deaths, marriages, illnesses and recoveries, gains and losses in the family and the kin, contain from the Circle and from the void. Let them ask the Circle for continuation and for good, and deliverance from the void.
63. And if you have not brought children of the body into the world, you have not continued what you could, and you have deprived continuation of what could have been, and you have stopped what is priceless: is this not void and non-being?
64. Or if you have not taught the children of the heart, you have not continued, and your words have died within you, and a part of the world has not been created or continued: is this not void and non-being?
65. The children of the body and the children of the heart are those who continue the parents and teachers. Are they not more important than all other things? For if there is no continuation, there is the void; who will continue your word and the world, who will repeat your Name?
66. Truly, when a woman brings a child into the world, she already continues the Circle; children are the foundation of the Circle of continuation of humanity, and life, and the creation of the world, and the continuation of the Circle, and there can be no excess in this.
67. Therefore, one who has not brought children of the body and heart into the world has spent in the void what they possessed; but if, having children, they have not brought them to the Circle, and left them without names, and not awakened them to the Path and continuation, is this not the void? They do not know.
68. The void is greedy for the one brought into the world; striking the one brought, it devours and remains. The one who has kept the child safe from the void is truly in continuation.
69. Therefore, ask the Circle to protect them even when they are in the womb, and let them hear.
70. Therefore, let the first words you speak to the newborn, when you first touch them, be words from the Circle of Being. For you are in the Circle, and you greet them, and you share what you have with them, and the Circle will descend upon them. The Circle, which is All, receives and preserves Your.
71. Therefore, do not delay Reunion and the finding of the Name for the newborn: for Reunion with the Circle is the supreme protection and the highest initiation, turning all previous and subsequent initiations into union with the Circle, and any signs into signs of the Circle. And behold, the one reunited with the Circle will not be taken as a sacrifice to the forms of god of the servants, though they will cunningly scheme!
72. Let the day of the finding of the Name in the Circle become a celebration for the newborn, and on this day, gift your child from the Circle of Being, and read the Book, and explain it so that they hear, for the Circle is in them and the Circle is in you, and truly, you pass to them from the Circle, and truly, you are alive.
73. And when they first call to the Circle from the depth of their heart, they will find the Call, and Discernment, and the Path, and let them know this.
74. And behold, you have protected and continued.
75. And if a servant has come near the newborn, you are the protector in the Circle, and did you not give the newborn the best protection and help? For they were born in the Circle, and by this their covenant with the Circle of Being is clearly sealed, and the beginning of all is one, and initiations without decision and Discernment lead to the void. Let the servant depart and seek no sacrifice here: truly, you must guard the continuation and life.
76. Honor and care for your father and mother, and their fathers and mothers, and the elders, and ancestors, and those with them, for you were born in the Circle through them, and the Circle is the father of you all.
77. You are the branch, they are the trunk; who does not care for their parents and ancestors is a broken branch: its fruit withers, and its core rots. For the one born is part of the continuation of the parent, and the one who cares for their beginning cares for their continuation.
78. And if you do not speak their Names, do you not continue? Truly, you are their continuation, and if their Names sound within you, then the elders are with you, and the born are with them.
79. And if an elder is deprived of care, it is a shame for their children and kin, for in them is void and scarcity, and they do not return what they have taken. Let them know this, and to them is the void. The one who has given care has truly avoided the void and continued, and will be rewarded, and has become continuation, and let them know this.
80. And those who are with you in the kin, are they not continuation to one another? The one who does not care for their own is like a distant branch: the wind will break it. If you do not serve one another with what is yours, and are not caring, and not thankful, and do not guard your own from the void, and are proud of abundance, and do not enter houses with good, and do not extend a hand to one another, then you have no kin and have not continued what you could, and before the void, decay. Thus, the whole kin is continuation.
81. And if your kin had a book of Names, where the Names could be called upon, and where the elders wrote to the younger, and gave it to each family in the kin, and united them, truly, this would be your great treasure and continuation, and knowledge, and the elders with you. Perhaps you would hear.
